    <!-- START js-modal-media -->
    <script type="text/javascript">
     var galleryBackBtn = 'Back'
		var galleryLocale = 'en_US';
		var pageEditMode = false;
		var urlOrigin = "https://www.melia.com";

		function openModalMedia(options) {
			var options = options || {};
			var $link = $("</a>").data(options);
			$(document).trigger('modalMedia.open', $link);
		}

		function closeModalMedia() {
			$(document).trigger('modalMedia.close');
		}

		function loadingGaleria(estado) {
			if (estado == "on") {
				$('body').addClass('loading');
				var capa = document.createElement("div");
				capa.id = "mbe-loader";
				code = '<div class="spinner">';
				code += '  <div class="dot1"></div>';
				code += '  <div class="dot2"></div>';
				code += '</div">';
				document.getElementsByTagName("body")[0].appendChild(capa);
				$('body #mbe-loader').append(code);
				// Se controla la tecla escape por si alguien la pulsa que no se quede la pagina bloqueada en el loading
				document.onkeydown = function (evt) {
					evt = evt || window.event;
					if (evt.keyCode == 27) {
						loading("off")
					}
				};
			} else {
				if (document.getElementById("mbe-loader") != undefined && document.getElementById("mbe-loader").parentNode.id == "loginTemplateremove") {
					document.getElementById("mbe-loader").remove();
				}
				document.getElementsByTagName("body")[0].removeChild(document.getElementById("mbe-loader"));
				$('body').removeClass('loading');
				// Anulado control de la tecla escape
				document.onkeydown = null;
			}
			return false;
		}

		if (typeof loading == "undefined") {
			loading = function (estado) {
				if (estado == "on") {
					$('body').addClass('loading');
					var capa = document.createElement("div");
					capa.id = "mbe-loader";
					code = '<div class="spinner">';
					code += '  <div class="dot1"></div>';
					code += '  <div class="dot2"></div>';
					code += '</div">';
					document.getElementsByTagName("body")[0].appendChild(capa);
					$('body #mbe-loader').append(code);
					// Se controla la tecla escape por si alguien la pulsa que no se quede la pagina bloqueada en el loading
					document.onkeydown = function (evt) {
						evt = evt || window.event;
						if (evt.keyCode == 27) {
							loading("off")
						}
					};
				} else {
					document.getElementsByTagName("body")[0].removeChild(document.getElementById("mbe-loader"));
					$('body').removeClass('loading');
					// Anulado control de la tecla escape
					document.onkeydown = null;
				}
				return false;
			}
		}

		var loadGallery;

		$(document).ready(function() {
			var $modalMedia = $("#modal-media");
			var $navTabs = $modalMedia.find(".nav-tabs");
			var $tabContent = $modalMedia.find(".tab-content");
			var $galleryIntro = $modalMedia.find(".grid-gallery-intro");
			var $galleryWrapper = $modalMedia.find(".grid-gallery-wrapper");
			var $galleryVideoWrapper = $modalMedia.find(".grid-gallery-video-wrapper");
			var $sociallinks = $modalMedia.find(".list-share");
			var $lastLink = "<a />";

			var hotelCode;

			// Carousel
			var SwipeCarrousel = {
				init: function (elements) {
					$(elements).each(function () {
						SwipeCarrousel.addSwipeSupport.call(this);
					});
				},
				addSwipeSupport: function () {
					$(this).swiperight(function () { $(this).carousel('prev') }).swipeleft(function () { $(this).carousel('next') });
				}
			};
			SwipeCarrousel.init($('.carousel'));

			var PauseCarousel = {
				init: function (elements) {
					$(elements).each(function () {
						$(this).carousel({
							pause: true,
							interval: false
						})
					})
				}
			}
			//  PauseCarousel.init($('.carousel'));

			var currentModalId = null;

			var showModalPage = function (page) {
				/*
					page = 1: vista inicial de imagenes, video o tour
					page = 2: seccion
					page = 3: galeria
					page = 4: detalle video o tour
				*/
				switch (page) {
					case 1:
						$tabContent.slideDown("slow");
						$galleryIntro.slideUp("slow");
						$galleryWrapper.slideUp("slow");
						$galleryVideoWrapper.slideUp("slow");
						break;
					case 2:
						$tabContent.slideUp("slow");
						$galleryIntro.slideDown("slow");
						$galleryWrapper.slideUp("slow");
						$galleryVideoWrapper.slideUp("slow");
						break;
					case 3:
						$tabContent.slideUp("slow");
						$galleryIntro.slideUp("slow");
						$galleryWrapper.slideDown("slow");
						$galleryVideoWrapper.slideUp("slow");
						break;
					case 4:
						$tabContent.slideUp("slow");
						$galleryIntro.slideUp("slow");
						$galleryWrapper.slideUp("slow");
						$galleryVideoWrapper.slideDown("slow");
						break;
				}
			};

			var openModalIfClosed = function (relatedTarget) {
				var isOpen = ($modalMedia.data('bs.modal') || { isShown: false }).isShown;
				if (!isOpen) {
					$modalMedia.modal('show', relatedTarget);
				}
			};

			var showTab = function (tabNumber) {
				$navTabs.find("a[href='#tab-" + tabNumber + "']").tab('show');
			};

			$('button.close').click(function () {
				$galleryVideoWrapper.children("div").empty();
			});

			$(".galleryClickListener").on("mouseenter", "article.hotel-article", function (event) {
				var codigoHotel = $(this).attr("id");
				if (typeof codigoHotel !== "undefined") {
					if (typeof jsonMediaGallery === "undefined" || jsonMediaGallery.length === 0 || (typeof jsonMediaGallery !== "undefined" && jsonMediaGallery.length > 0 && typeof jsonMediaGallery[0].name !== "undefined" && jsonMediaGallery[0].name.split("_").length > 1 && jsonMediaGallery[0].name.split("_")[0] !== codigoHotel)) {
						$.ajax({
							async: true,
							url: urlOrigin + "/.rest/magnolia-mhi-hotelfactsheet-module/v1/template/rest-json-gallery?content=/" + codigoHotel,
							type: "GET"
						});
					}
				}
			});

			/* Handler que abre el modal */
			var rulesCityDSK = ".c-hotel-content .div-image.galleryClickListener";
			var rulesBannerHotelDSK = ".c-hotel-sheet-hero .galleryClickListener";
			var rulesRoomListDSK = ".c-hotel-sheet-room .div-image";
			var rulesSectionListDSK = ".c-hotel-sheet-info-description.c-hotel-sheet-list .description-foto";
			var rulesDetailImgDSK = ".c-hotel-sheet-detail .c-hotel-sheet-detail__img";
			var rulesMosaicDSK = ".c-hotel-sheet-images-6 .img-container.grid-item, .c-hotel-sheet-images-4 .img-container.grid-item, .c-hotel-sheet-images-6 .galleryClickListener .btn-container.btn-footer.btn-big-icons, .c-hotel-sheet-images-4 .galleryClickListener .btn-container.btn-footer.btn-big-icons";
			var rulesBookingDSK = "#hotelesDisp .mod-ficha-hotel .ficha-hotel-content .div-image";
			var rulesBookingRATES = ".hotel .div-image .galleryClickListener";
			var rulesDESKTOP = rulesCityDSK+", "+rulesBannerHotelDSK+", "+rulesRoomListDSK+", "+rulesSectionListDSK+", "+rulesDetailImgDSK+", "+rulesMosaicDSK+", "+rulesBookingDSK+", "+rulesBookingRATES;

			var rulesCityAMP = ".c-room__content .c-room__image.c-hotel-list";
			var rulesBannerHotelAMP = ".c-hotel-hero .galleryClickListener";
			var rulesSectionListAMP = ".c-room__content .c-room__image.c-hotel-section-list";
			var rulesDetailImgAMP = ".c-intro-brand .u-relative";
			var rulesMosaicAMP = ".c-hotel-visual-tour .c-hotel-visual-tour__video, .c-hotel-visual-tour .c-hotel-visual-tour__photos, .c-hotel-visual-tour .c-hotel-visual-tour__buttons .c-hotel-visual-tour__button.galleryClickListener";
			var rulesBookingAMP = ".c-list-hotels-hotel .photo.galleryClickListener";
			var rulesAMP = rulesCityAMP+", "+rulesBannerHotelAMP+", "+rulesSectionListAMP+", "+rulesDetailImgAMP+", "+rulesMosaicAMP+", "+rulesBookingAMP;

			var rulesMODAL = "#modal-media .modal-content .breadcrumb li:not(.active), #modal-media .tab-pane.active .media-wrapper, #modal-media .grid-gallery-intro .media-wrapper";

			$(document).on("click", rulesDESKTOP+", "+rulesAMP+", "+rulesMODAL, function (event) {
				aMediaGalleryBtn = true;
				if ($(this).hasClass("btn-big-icons")) {
					$lastLink = $(event.target);
				} else {
					$lastLink = $(this).find(".mediaGalleryBtn");
				}
				var codigoHotel = $(this).find(".mediaGalleryBtn").attr("data-load-hotel");
				var nameHotelNormalizado = $(this).find(".mediaGalleryBtn").attr("data-hotel-title");
				if (typeof codigoHotel !== "undefined") {
					if (typeof jsonMediaGallery === "undefined" || jsonMediaGallery.length === 0 || (typeof jsonMediaGallery !== "undefined" && jsonMediaGallery.length > 0 && typeof jsonMediaGallery[0].name !== "undefined" && jsonMediaGallery[0].name.split("_").length > 1 && jsonMediaGallery[0].name.split("_")[0] !== codigoHotel)) {
						loading("on");
						$.ajax({
							async: true,
							url: urlOrigin + "/.rest/magnolia-mhi-hotelfactsheet-module/v1/template/rest-json-gallery?content=/" + nameHotelNormalizado,
							type: "GET",
						success: function (galeriaUnformatted) {
								try {
								if(typeof galeriaUnformatted === 'object' && galeriaUnformatted !== null){
									jsonMediaGallery = createJsonMediaGallery(galeriaUnformatted);
									loadGallery();
									loading("off");
								}
								} catch (e) {
									loading("off");
								}
							},
							error: function (res) {
								loading("off");
							}
						});
					} else {
						loadGallery();
					}
				} else if (typeof codigoHotelFicha !== "undefined" && codigoHotelFicha.length > 0 && (typeof jsonMediaGallery === "undefined" || jsonMediaGallery.length === 0)) {
					loading("on");
					$.ajax({
						async: true,
						url: urlOrigin + "/.rest/magnolia-mhi-hotelfactsheet-module/v1/template/rest-json-gallery?content=/" + nameHotelNormalizado,
						type: "GET",
					success: function (galeriaUnformatted) {
							try {
							if(typeof galeriaUnformatted === 'object' && galeriaUnformatted !== null){
								jsonMediaGallery = createJsonMediaGallery(galeriaUnformatted);
								loadGallery();
								loading("off");
							}
							} catch (e) {
								loading("off");
							}
						},
						error: function (res) {
							loading("off");
						}
					});
				} else {
					loadGallery();
				}
				aMediaGalleryBtn = false;
			});

			$(".galleryClickListener").on('modalMedia.open', function (event, $link) {
				openModal($link);
			});

			$(".galleryClickListener").on('modalMedia.close', function (event, $link) {
				$modalMedia.modal('hide');
				$('#youtubePlayer')[0].contentWindow.postMessage('{"event":"command","func":"' + 'stopVideo' + '","args":""}', '*');
			});

			loadGallery = function () {
				if (typeof jsonMediaGallery === "undefined") {
					jsonMediaGallery = [];
				}

				// Oculta las tabs que no tengan contenido.
				var tabImages = false;
				var tabVideos = false;
				var tabTour = false;

				for (i in jsonMediaGallery) {
					if (typeof jsonMediaGallery[i].name !== "undefined" && typeof jsonMediaGallery[i].content !== "undefined" && jsonMediaGallery[i].content.length > 0) {
						if (jsonMediaGallery[i].name.indexOf("imagenes") > -1) {
							tabImages = true;
							$navTabs.find('a[href="#tab-fotos"]').parent().show();
						} else if (jsonMediaGallery[i].name.indexOf("videos") > -1) {
							tabVideos = true;
							$navTabs.find('a[href="#tab-videos"]').parent().show();
						} else if (jsonMediaGallery[i].name.indexOf("tour_virtual") > -1) {
							tabTour = true;
							$navTabs.find('a[href="#tab-virtual-tour"]').parent().show();
						}
					}
				}

				if (!tabImages) {
					$navTabs.find('a[href="#tab-fotos"]').parent().hide();
					// Quitar botón del mosaico "fotos".
					$(".mediaGalleryBtn[data-modal-media-tab='fotos']").hide();
				}

				if (!tabVideos) {
					$navTabs.find('a[href="#tab-videos"]').parent().hide();
					// Quitar botón del mosaico "videos".
					$(".mediaGalleryBtn[data-modal-media-tab='videos']").hide();
				}

				if (!tabTour) {
					$navTabs.find('a[href="#tab-virtual-tour"]').parent().hide();
					// Quitar botón del mosaico "virtual-tour".
					$(".mediaGalleryBtn[data-modal-media-tab='virtual-tour']").hide();
				}

				if (!$modalMedia.hasClass("in")) {
					$("div.grid-media").remove();
				}

				$sociallinks.hide();

				if (jsonMediaGallery.length > 0 && typeof jsonMediaGallery[0].parent !== "undefined") {
					$("#titulo_hotel").val(jsonMediaGallery[0].parent);
				} else {
					$("#titulo_hotel").val("");
				}
				openModal();

				// SwipeCarrousel.init($('.carousel'));
				$('.carousel').carousel();
				if (typeof hotel_location !== "undefined") {
					if ((typeof $(this).attr("data-url") === "undefined") || $(this).attr("data-url") === "") {
						hotel_location = location.href;
					} else {
						hotel_location = location.href.split("/")[0] + "//" + location.href.split("/")[2] + $(this).attr("data-url");
					}
					$('ul.list-inline.list-share a').slice(0, 3).attr('href', function () { return this.href.slice(0, this.href.indexOf("=") + 1) + hotel_location; });
				}
			}

			var openModal = function ($link) {
				if (typeof $link === "undefined") {
					$link = $lastLink;
				}
				openModalIfClosed($link);

				var data;
				if(typeof $link.data() !== "object" && $link.hasOwnProperty("context")) {
				    data = $link.context.dataset;
				} else {
				    data = $link.data();
				}

				var sectionName = data.loadName;
				var obj = encontrarSeccion(jsonMediaGallery, sectionName);
				if ((typeof obj === "undefined" || obj.value === null || typeof obj.value.content === "undefined" || obj.value.content.length === 0) && $link.hasClass("restaurantGalleryBtn")) {
					var code = sectionName.split("_");
					if (code.length > 1) {
						obj = encontrarSeccion(jsonMediaGallery, code[0] + "_restaurantes");
					}
				}
				var media = "";
				if (typeof obj.order !== "undefined" && obj.order.length > 0 && jsonMediaGallery.length > obj.order[0]) {
					var mediaName = jsonMediaGallery[obj.order[0]].name.split("_");
					if (mediaName.length > 0) {
						media = mediaName[mediaName.length - 1];
					}
				}
				var resultado = rellenarSeccion(obj);
				var showModalPageNumber = 1;
				if (typeof obj.value !== "undefined" && obj.value !== null && typeof obj.order !== "undefined") {
					if (typeof obj.value.depth !== "undefined" && typeof obj.value.content !== "undefined" && media.length > 0) {
						$('#carousel-media').remove();
						switch (media) {
							case 'virtual':
								if (obj.value.depth === obj.order.length) {
									$("#tab-virtual-tour").html(resultado);
									showModalPageNumber = 1;
								} else if (obj.value.depth < obj.order.length) {
									$galleryVideoWrapper.html(resultado);
									$sociallinks.hide();
									showModalPageNumber = 4;
								}
								showTab("virtual-tour");
								break;
							case 'videos':
								if (obj.value.depth === obj.order.length) {
									$("#tab-videos").html(resultado);
									showModalPageNumber = 1;
								} else if (obj.value.depth < obj.order.length) {
									$galleryVideoWrapper.html(resultado);
									$sociallinks.hide();
									showModalPageNumber = 4;
								}
								showTab("videos");
								break;
							default:
								if (obj.value.depth === 1) {
									$("#tab-fotos").html(resultado);
									showModalPageNumber = 1;
								} else if ((obj.value.depth === 2 && obj.value.content.length > 0 && typeof obj.value.content[0].content === "undefined") || obj.value.depth === 3) {
									$galleryWrapper.html(resultado);
									$galleryWrapper.append($sociallinks);
									$galleryWrapper.find(".list-share").show();
									updateCarouselCount();
									showModalPageNumber = 3;
								} else {
									$galleryIntro.html(resultado);
									showModalPageNumber = 2;
								}
								showTab("fotos");
						}
					} else {
						$("#tab-fotos").html("");
						$("#tab-videos").html("");
						$("#tab-virtual-tour").html("");
					}
				} else {
					$("#tab-fotos").html("");
					$("#tab-videos").html("");
					$("#tab-virtual-tour").html("");
				}
				showModalPage(showModalPageNumber);
			};

			$navTabs.find('a[data-toggle="tab"]').on('shown.bs.tab', function (e) {
				// aMediaGalleryBtn --> Para evitar que entre cuando se carga la galería por primera vez.
				if (!aMediaGalleryBtn) {
					var media = $(this).attr("href").split("-")[1];
					var codigoHotel = "";
					if (typeof jsonMediaGallery !== "undefined" && jsonMediaGallery.length > 0 && typeof jsonMediaGallery[0].name !== "undefined") {
						var nameParts = jsonMediaGallery[0].name.split("_");
						if (nameParts.length > 1) {
							codigoHotel = nameParts[0] + "_";
						}
					}
					$galleryVideoWrapper.children("div").empty();
					var resultado = "";
					var obj = "";
					switch (media) {
						case 'virtual': obj = encontrarSeccion(jsonMediaGallery, codigoHotel + "tour_virtual"); resultado = rellenarSeccion(obj); $("#tab-virtual-tour").html(resultado); break;
						case 'videos': obj = encontrarSeccion(jsonMediaGallery, codigoHotel + "videos"); resultado = rellenarSeccion(obj); $("#tab-videos").html(resultado); break;
						default: obj = encontrarSeccion(jsonMediaGallery, codigoHotel + "imagenes"); resultado = rellenarSeccion(obj); $("#tab-fotos").html(resultado);
					}
					showModalPage(1);
				}
			});

			var updateCarouselCount = function () {
				var $carouselMedia = $('.grid-gallery-wrapper #carousel-media');
				var $items = $carouselMedia.find(".item");
				var currentIndex = $items.index($items.filter(".active"));
				var total = $items.length;
				var text = (currentIndex + 1) + " / " + total;
				$('.carousel-media-counter').text(text);
			};

			$(".galleryClickListener").on('slid.bs.carousel', '#carousel-media', updateCarouselCount);
		});


		function encontrarSeccion(obj, name) {
			// out.order = Array con la posición en cada nivel del json de la sección o imagen de la galeria a mostrar. La posición menor de array indica la posición en el nivel más alto del arbol.
			// out.value = Objeto json de la sección concreta que se va a mostrar en la galeria
			var out = { "order": [], "value": null };

			//Se encargar de rellenar el objeto out.
			$.each(obj, function (i, v) {
				if (v.name === name) {
					out.value = v;
					Array.prototype.unshift.call(out.order, i);
					return false; // stops the loop
				}
				if (typeof v.content !== "undefined") {
					var r = encontrarSeccion(v.content, name);
					if (r.value !== null) {
						out = r;
						Array.prototype.unshift.call(out.order, i);
						return false;
					}
				}
			});
			return out;
		}


		function rellenarSeccion(obj) {
			obj = rellenarImagenYContador(obj);
			var resultado = '';
			if (typeof obj !== "undefined" && typeof obj.value !== "undefined" && obj.value !== null && typeof obj.value.content !== "undefined") {
				if (/^(_|\d)*videos$/.test(obj.value.name) || /^(_|\d)*tour_virtual$/.test(obj.value.name)) {
					var isElement = false;
					var element = 0;
					if (obj.order.length > obj.value.depth) {
						isElement = true;
						element = obj.order[obj.order.length - 1];
					}
					if (isElement) {
						resultado += '<ol class="breadcrumb"><li><a href="javascript:void(0)" class="mediaGalleryBtn" data-load-name="' + jsonMediaGallery[obj.order[0]].name + '">' + galleryBackBtn + '</a></li><li class="active">' + obj.value.content[element].title + '</li></ol>';
						if (typeof pageEditMode !== "undefined" && pageEditMode === "true") {
							resultado += '<div style="text-align: center;"><a href="' + obj.value.content[element].urledit + '" target="_blank">' + obj.value.content[element].botonedit + '</a></div><div class="video-responsive"><iframe id="youtubePlayer" width="560" height="315" src="' + objJSONMediaGallery.videos[i].content[x].urlvideo + '" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen="true" allowscriptaccess="always"></iframe></div>';
						}
						resultado += '<div class="video-responsive"><iframe id="youtubePlayer" width="560" height="315" src="' + obj.value.content[element].url + '" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen="true" allowscriptaccess="always"></iframe></div>';
					} else {
						if (/^(_|\d)*videos$/.test(obj.value.name)) {
							resultado += '<div class="row grid-media grid-videos">';
						} else {
							resultado += '<div class="row grid-media grid-virtual-tour">';
						}
						if (typeof obj.value.content !== "undefined") {
							for (var a = 0; a < obj.value.content.length; a++) {
								if (a % 3 === 0) {
									resultado += '<div class="clearfix visible-sm"></div>';
								}
								if (a !== 0 && a % 4 === 0) {
									resultado += '<div class="clearfix visible-md visible-lg"></div>';
								}
								resultado += '<div class="col-sm-4 col-md-3"><div class="media-wrapper"><a class="mediaGalleryBtn" href="javascript:void(0)" data-load-name="' + obj.value.content[a].name + '"><img class="img-responsive" src="' + obj.value.content[a].image + '" /><span class="media-icon"><i class="icon-video"></i></span></a></div><h5 class="h3"><a class="mediaGalleryBtn" href="javascript:void(0)" data-load-name="' + obj.value.content[a].name + '">' + obj.value.content[a].title + '</a></h5></div>';
							}
						}
						resultado += '</div>';
					}
				} else {
					// Si el array de posición en el árbol tiene más niveles que la profundidad de la sección es que se ha introducido una imagen. Se marca esta imagen para que se muestre al abrir la galeria
					var active = 0;
					if (obj.order.length > obj.value.depth) {
						active = obj.order[obj.order.length - 1];
					}
					var c = 0;
					for (var y = 0; y < obj.value.content.length; y++) {
						if (typeof obj.value.content[y].content === "undefined") {
							if (y === 0) {
								resultado += '<ol class="breadcrumb"><li><a href="javascript:void(0)" class="mediaGalleryBtn" data-load-name="' + ((obj.value.depth > 2) ? jsonMediaGallery[obj.order[0]].content[obj.order[1]].name : jsonMediaGallery[obj.order[0]].name) + '">' + galleryBackBtn + '</a></li><li class="active">' + ((obj.value.depth === 1) ? obj.value.parent : obj.value.title) + ' <span class="carousel-media-counter"></span></li></ol><div id="carousel-media" class="carousel slide" data-ride="carousel"><div oncontextmenu="return false;" class="carousel-inner" role="listbox">';
							}
							if (y === active) {
								resultado += '<div class="item active">';
							} else {
								resultado += '<div class="item">';
							}
							if (typeof pageEditMode !== "undefined" && pageEditMode === "true") {
								resultado += '<div style="text-align: center;"><a href="' + obj.value.content[y].urledit + '" target=_blank>' + obj.value.content[y].botonedit + '</a></div>';
							}
							resultado += '<img src="' + obj.value.content[y].url + '" /></div>';
							if (y === obj.value.content.length - 1 && obj.value.content.length > 1) {
								resultado += '</div><a onclick="stopmiddleclick(window.event)" oncontextmenu="return false;" class="left carousel-control" href="#carousel-media" role="button" data-slide="prev"><span aria-hidden="true"><i class="icon-left-arrow"></i></span><span class="sr-only">Previous</span></a><a onclick="stopmiddleclick(window.event)" oncontextmenu="return false;" class="right carousel-control" href="#carousel-media" role="button" data-slide="next"><span aria-hidden="true"><i class="icon-right-arrow"></i></span><span class="sr-only">Next</span></a></div>';
							}
						} else {
							if (y === 0) {
								resultado += '<ol class="breadcrumb">';
								if (obj.value.depth !== 1) {
									resultado += '<li><a href="javascript:void(0)" class="mediaGalleryBtn" data-load-name="' + jsonMediaGallery[obj.order[0]].name + '" >' + galleryBackBtn + '</a></li>';
								}
								resultado += '<li class="active">' + ((obj.value.depth === 1) ? obj.value.parent : obj.value.title) + '</li></ol><div class="row grid-media">';
							}
							if (obj.value.content[y].meter > 0) {
								if (c % 3 === 0) {
									resultado += '<div class="clearfix visible-sm"></div>';
								}
								if (c !== 0 && c % 4 === 0) {
									resultado += '<div class="clearfix visible-md visible-lg"></div>';
								}
								resultado += '<div class="col-sm-4 col-md-3"><div class="media-wrapper"><a class="mediaGalleryBtn" href="javascript:void(0)" data-load-name="' + obj.value.content[y].name + '"><img class="img-responsive" src="' + obj.value.content[y].image + '" /><span class="media-icon">' + obj.value.content[y].meter + '<i class="icon-camera"></i></span></a></div><h5 class="h3"><a class="mediaGalleryBtn" href="javascript:void(0)" data-load-name="' + obj.value.content[y].name + '">' + obj.value.content[y].title + '</a></h5></div>';
								c++;
							}
							if (y === obj.value.content.length - 1) {
								resultado += '</div>';
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			return resultado;
		}


		function rellenarImagenYContador(obj) {
			// Si out.value es un contenido (imagen, video o tour) lo sustituye con la sección que lo contiene. En obj.order sigue estando la posición del contenido como último valor.
			var json = jsonMediaGallery;
			if (typeof obj.value !== "undefined" && obj.value !== null) {
				if (typeof obj.value.content === "undefined") {
					for (var i = 0; i < obj.order.length; i++) {
						if (typeof json[obj.order[i]].content !== "undefined") {
							obj.value = json[obj.order[i]];
						}
						json = json[obj.order[i]].content;
					}
				}
				if (typeof obj.value.content !== "undefined") {
					// Se analiza la profundidad de la sección para establece qué categoria buscar.
					var category = "";
					if (obj.value.depth === 1) {
						category = "Destacado_Raiz_Galeria";
					} else if (obj.value.depth === 2) {
						category = "Destacado_Detalle_Galeria";
					}
					var subCategory = "Destacado_Detalle_Galeria";
					var meter; //variable que almacena el número de contenidos por sección para el contador
					// Se itera la sección para buscar los contenidos setear el contador y la imagen de detalle.
					for (var a = 0; a < obj.value.content.length; a++) {
						if (typeof obj.value.content[a].content !== "undefined") {
							meter = 0;
							var subImage = "";
							for (var b = 0; b < obj.value.content[a].content.length; b++) {
								if (typeof obj.value.content[a].content[b].content !== "undefined") {
									for (var c = 0; c < obj.value.content[a].content[b].content.length; c++) {
										if (typeof urlNotAvaliableImage === "undefined" || urlNotAvaliableImage.length === 0 || (typeof obj.value.content[a].content[b].content[c].url !== "undefined" && obj.value.content[a].content[b].content[c].url.indexOf(urlNotAvaliableImage) === -1)) {
											if (typeof obj.value.content[a].content[b].content[c].categories !== "undefined" && obj.value.content[a].content[b].content[c].categories.indexOf(category) >= 0 && typeof obj.value.content[a].content[b].content[c].url !== "undefined" && category.length > 0) {
												obj.value.content[a].image = obj.value.content[a].content[b].content[c].url;
											}
											if (subImage.length === 0 && typeof obj.value.content[a].content[b].content[c].categories !== "undefined" && obj.value.content[a].content[b].content[c].categories.indexOf(subCategory) >= 0 && typeof obj.value.content[a].content[b].content[c].url !== "undefined" && subCategory.length > 0) {
												subImage = obj.value.content[a].content[b].content[c].url;
											}
											meter++;
										} else {
											obj.value.content[a].content[b].content.splice(c, 1);
										}
									}
								} else {
									if (typeof urlNotAvaliableImage === "undefined" || urlNotAvaliableImage.length === 0 || (typeof obj.value.content[a].content[b].url !== "undefined" && obj.value.content[a].content[b].url.indexOf(urlNotAvaliableImage) === -1)) {
										if (typeof obj.value.content[a].content[b].categories !== "undefined" && obj.value.content[a].content[b].categories.indexOf(category) >= 0 && typeof obj.value.content[a].content[b].url !== "undefined" && category.length > 0) {
											obj.value.content[a].image = obj.value.content[a].content[b].url;
										}
										if (subImage.length === 0 && typeof obj.value.content[a].content[b].categories !== "undefined" && obj.value.content[a].content[b].categories.indexOf(subCategory) >= 0 && typeof obj.value.content[a].content[b].url !== "undefined" && subCategory.length > 0) {
											subImage = obj.value.content[a].content[b].url;
										}
										meter++;
									} else {
										obj.value.content[a].content.splice(b, 1);
									}
								}
								if (typeof obj.value.content[a].image === "undefined" || obj.value.content[a].image.length === 0) {
									obj.value.content[a].image = subImage;
								}
							}
							obj.value.content[a].meter = meter;
						} else {
							if (typeof urlNotAvaliableImage !== "undefined" && urlNotAvaliableImage.length > 0 && (typeof obj.value.content[a].url === "undefined" || obj.value.content[a].url.indexOf(urlNotAvaliableImage) > -1)) {
								obj.value.content.splice(a, 1);
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			return obj;
		}
	
	
		function stopmiddleclick(e) {
			//var rightclick;
			if (!e || e === undefined || e === false){
				var e = window.event;
			}
			if (e.which == 2){
				e.stopPropagation();
				e.preventDefault();
				e.stopImmediatePropagation();
				return false;
			}
		}


		//disable right click
		$(".disabledrightclick").bind('contextmenu', function(e) {
			e.stopPropagation();
			e.preventDefault();
			e.stopImmediatePropagation();
			return false;
		});


		+function ($) {
			'use strict';

			// TAB CLASS DEFINITION
			// ====================

			var Tab = function (element) {
				// jscs:disable requireDollarBeforejQueryAssignment
				this.element = $(element)
				// jscs:enable requireDollarBeforejQueryAssignment
			}

			Tab.VERSION = '3.3.5'
			Tab.TRANSITION_DURATION = 150

			Tab.prototype.show = function () {
				var $this = this.element
				var $ul = $this.closest('ul:not(.dropdown-menu)')
				var selector = $this.data('target')

				if (!selector) {
					selector = $this.attr('href')
					selector = selector && selector.replace(/.*(?=#[^\s]*$)/, '') // strip for ie7
				}

				if ($this.parent('li').hasClass('active')) return

				var $previous = $ul.find('.active:last a')
				var hideEvent = $.Event('hide.bs.tab', {
					relatedTarget: $this[0]
				})
				var showEvent = $.Event('show.bs.tab', {
					relatedTarget: $previous[0]
				})

				$previous.trigger(hideEvent)
				$this.trigger(showEvent)

				if (showEvent.isDefaultPrevented() || hideEvent.isDefaultPrevented()) return

				var $target = $(selector)

				this.activate($this.closest('li'), $ul)
				this.activate($target, $target.parent(), function () {
					$previous.trigger({
						type: 'hidden.bs.tab',
						relatedTarget: $this[0]
					})
					$this.trigger({
						type: 'shown.bs.tab',
						relatedTarget: $previous[0]
					})
				})
			}

			Tab.prototype.activate = function (element, container, callback) {
				var $active = container.find('> .active')
				var transition = callback
					&& $.support.transition
					&& ($active.length && $active.hasClass('fade') || !!container.find('> .fade').length)

				function next() {
					$active
						.removeClass('active')
						.find('> .dropdown-menu > .active')
						.removeClass('active')
						.end()
						.find('[data-toggle="tab"]')
						.attr('aria-expanded', false)

					element
						.addClass('active')
						.find('[data-toggle="tab"]')
						.attr('aria-expanded', true)

					if (transition) {
						element[0].offsetWidth // reflow for transition
						element.addClass('in')
					} else {
						element.removeClass('fade')
					}

					if (element.parent('.dropdown-menu').length) {
						element
							.closest('li.dropdown')
							.addClass('active')
							.end()
							.find('[data-toggle="tab"]')
							.attr('aria-expanded', true)
					}
	
					callback && callback()
				}

				$active.length && transition ?
					$active
						.one('bsTransitionEnd', next)
						.emulateTransitionEnd(Tab.TRANSITION_DURATION) :
					next()
	
				$active.removeClass('in')
			}

			// TAB PLUGIN DEFINITION
			// =====================
			function Plugin(option) {
				return this.each(function () {
					var $this = $(this)
					var data = $this.data('bs.tab')
					if (!data) $this.data('bs.tab', (data = new Tab(this)))
					if (typeof option == 'string') data[option]()
				})
			}

			var old = $.fn.tab
			$.fn.tab = Plugin
			$.fn.tab.Constructor = Tab

			// TAB NO CONFLICT
			// ===============
			$.fn.tab.noConflict = function () {
				$.fn.tab = old
				return this
			}

			// TAB DATA-API
			// ============
			var clickHandler = function (e) {
				e.preventDefault()
				Plugin.call($(this), 'show')
			}

			$(".galleryClickListener").on('click.bs.tab.data-api', '[data-toggle="tab"]', clickHandler)
		}(jQuery);


		+function ($) {
			'use strict';

			// CAROUSEL CLASS DEFINITION
			// =========================

			var Carousel = function (element, options) {
				this.$element = $(element)
				this.$indicators = this.$element.find('.carousel-indicators')
				this.options = options
				this.paused = null
				this.sliding = null
				this.interval = null
				this.$active = null
				this.$items = null

				this.options.keyboard && this.$element.on('keydown.bs.carousel', $.proxy(this.keydown, this))

				this.options.pause == 'hover' && !('ontouchstart' in document.documentElement) && this.$element
					.on('mouseenter.bs.carousel', $.proxy(this.pause, this))
					.on('mouseleave.bs.carousel', $.proxy(this.cycle, this))
			}

			Carousel.VERSION = '3.3.5'
			Carousel.TRANSITION_DURATION = 600

			Carousel.DEFAULTS = {
				interval: 5000,
				pause: 'hover',
				wrap: true,
				keyboard: true
			}

			Carousel.prototype.keydown = function (e) {
				if (/input|textarea/i.test(e.target.tagName)) return
				switch (e.which) {
					case 37: this.prev(); break
					case 39: this.next(); break
					default: return
				}
				e.preventDefault()
			}

			Carousel.prototype.cycle = function (e) {
				e || (this.paused = false)
				this.interval && clearInterval(this.interval)
				this.options.interval
					&& !this.paused
					&& (this.interval = setInterval($.proxy(this.next, this), this.options.interval))
				return this
			}

			Carousel.prototype.getItemIndex = function (item) {
				this.$items = item.parent().children('.item')
				return this.$items.index(item || this.$active)
			}

			Carousel.prototype.getItemForDirection = function (direction, active) {
				var activeIndex = this.getItemIndex(active)
				var willWrap = (direction == 'prev' && activeIndex === 0)
					|| (direction == 'next' && activeIndex == (this.$items.length - 1))
				if (willWrap && !this.options.wrap) return active
				var delta = direction == 'prev' ? -1 : 1
				var itemIndex = (activeIndex + delta) % this.$items.length
				return this.$items.eq(itemIndex)
			}

			Carousel.prototype.to = function (pos) {
				var that = this
				var activeIndex = this.getItemIndex(this.$active = this.$element.find('.item.active'))
				if (pos > (this.$items.length - 1) || pos < 0) return
				if (this.sliding) return this.$element.one('slid.bs.carousel', function () { that.to(pos) }) // yes, "slid"
				if (activeIndex == pos) return this.pause().cycle()
				return this.slide(pos > activeIndex ? 'next' : 'prev', this.$items.eq(pos))
			}

			Carousel.prototype.pause = function (e) {
				e || (this.paused = true)
				if (this.$element.find('.next, .prev').length && $.support.transition) {
					this.$element.trigger($.support.transition.end)
					this.cycle(true)
				}
				this.interval = clearInterval(this.interval)
				return this
			}

			Carousel.prototype.next = function () {
				if (this.sliding) return
				return this.slide('next')
			}

			Carousel.prototype.prev = function () {
				if (this.sliding) return
				return this.slide('prev')
			}

			Carousel.prototype.slide = function (type, next) {
				var $active = this.$element.find('.item.active')
				var $next = next || this.getItemForDirection(type, $active)
				var isCycling = this.interval
				var direction = type == 'next' ? 'left' : 'right'
				var that = this

				if ($next.hasClass('active')) return (this.sliding = false)

				var relatedTarget = $next[0]
				var slideEvent = $.Event('slide.bs.carousel', {
					relatedTarget: relatedTarget,
					direction: direction
				})
				this.$element.trigger(slideEvent)

				if (slideEvent.isDefaultPrevented()) return
				this.sliding = true
				isCycling && this.pause()

				if (this.$indicators.length) {
					this.$indicators.find('.active').removeClass('active')
					var $nextIndicator = $(this.$indicators.children()[this.getItemIndex($next)])
					$nextIndicator && $nextIndicator.addClass('active')
				}

				var slidEvent = $.Event('slid.bs.carousel', { relatedTarget: relatedTarget, direction: direction }) // yes, "slid"
				if ($.support.transition && this.$element.hasClass('slide')) {
					$next.addClass(type)
					$next[0].offsetWidth // force reflow
					$active.addClass(direction)
					$next.addClass(direction)
					$active
						.one('bsTransitionEnd', function () {
							$next.removeClass([type, direction].join(' ')).addClass('active')
							$active.removeClass(['active', direction].join(' '))
							that.sliding = false
							setTimeout(function () {
								that.$element.trigger(slidEvent)
							}, 0)
						})
						.emulateTransitionEnd(Carousel.TRANSITION_DURATION)
				} else {
					$active.removeClass('active')
					$next.addClass('active')
					this.sliding = false
					this.$element.trigger(slidEvent)
				}

				isCycling && this.cycle()
				return this
			}

			// CAROUSEL PLUGIN DEFINITION
			// ==========================
			function Plugin(option) {
				return this.each(function () {
					var $this = $(this)
					var data = $this.data('bs.carousel')
					var options = $.extend({}, Carousel.DEFAULTS, $this.data(), typeof option == 'object' && option)
					var action = typeof option == 'string' ? option : options.slide

					if (!data) $this.data('bs.carousel', (data = new Carousel(this, options)))
					if (typeof option == 'number') data.to(option)
					else if (action) data[action]()
					else if (options.interval) data.pause().cycle()
				})
			}

			var old = $.fn.carousel

			$.fn.carousel = Plugin
			$.fn.carousel.Constructor = Carousel

			// CAROUSEL NO CONFLICT
			// ====================
			$.fn.carousel.noConflict = function () {
				$.fn.carousel = old
				return this
			}

			// CAROUSEL DATA-API
			// =================
			var clickHandler = function (e) {
				var href
				var $this = $(this)
				var $target = $($this.attr('data-target') || (href = $this.attr('href')) && href.replace(/.*(?=#[^\s]+$)/, '')) // strip for ie7
				if (!$target.hasClass('carousel')) return
				var options = $.extend({}, $target.data(), $this.data())
				var slideIndex = $this.attr('data-slide-to')
				if (slideIndex) options.interval = false

				Plugin.call($target, options)

				if (slideIndex) {
					$target.data('bs.carousel').to(slideIndex)
				}

				e.preventDefault()
			}

			$(".galleryClickListener").on('click.bs.carousel.data-api', '[data-slide]', clickHandler)

			$(window).on('load', function () {
				$('[data-ride="carousel"]').each(function () {
					var $carousel = $(this)
					Plugin.call($carousel, $carousel.data())
				})
			})

		}(jQuery);
    </script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
     $( document ).ready(function() {
	    var lang = $('html').attr('lang');
	    if(lang == 'null' || lang == undefined || lang == ''){
	    	lang = 'en_GB';
	    }
		$.ajax({
			url : "/booking/home/C_TopDestinosSIE.jsp?f=" +  new Date().getTime() + "&lang=" + lang,
			type: "POST",
			dataType: 'html',
			data: {},
			success : function(html) {
				$("#topDestinosHome").append(html);
			}
		});

	});
    </script>

We would also like to inform you that MELIÁ is responsible for its own and third-part cookies and the processing of data obtained through their use, as well as decisions regarding the purpose, content and use of the information collected.
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         What is a cookie?
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
        Cookies are files that contain small amounts of information that are downloaded to users’ devices when they visit a website. This allows us to technically identify information about a user and their device, without any need to directly process their personal data.
       </p>
       <p>
        Cookies are essential for making the Internet work. They cannot damage users’ devices and their activation in the browser settings can help identify and resolve possible errors in the way the Website works.
       </p>
       <p>
        Cookies have many purposes, such as making navigation between pages more efficient, remembering your preferences and, in general, collecting information on navigation in order to improve the user experience. They also help ensure that the ads you see online are the most relevant ads for you based on your preferences and interests.
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         How do we use cookies?
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
        By accepting cookies through the mechanisms enabled on the Website or by adjusting your cookie settings, you expressly accept the use of cookies on your devices. If you disable cookies, some of the functionality on the Website may not work properly.
       </p>
       <p>
        Specifically, at MELIÁ we use cookies for the purposes described below. If we use other cookies in the future to offer more and better services, we will inform users.
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         TECHNICAL COOKIES
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
        Technical cookies help users move around a website and use its functionality. In general, these cookies enable the different website functionality, make browsing more secure or provide functionalities that have been previously requested by users. As they are required for the operation of the Website, these cookies will be activated by default and their installation cannot be rejected.
       </p>
       <p>
        MELIÁ may use the cookies required to save your cookie preferences in our systems, stabilise your browsing or make it more secure.
       </p>

        To manage cookies, most browsers allow you to reject or accept all cookies or only accept certain types of cookies. The process for managing and deleting cookies can be found in the help section of your browser. If you would like to limit the use of cookies, it may not be possible to use all the interactive functionality on our Website.
       </p>
       <p>
        Cookies installed on your computer may be allowed, blocked or deleted by changing the browser options on your computer:
       </p>

  <script>
   function desplegarLogin(){
    
        loadCaptchaAPILogin(loadCaptchaLogin, 'en_us');
    
	$(".c-header__menu-login").css("display","block");
}

var interval;

$(document).ready(function(){
    initHome();
});

function initHome() {
    if(checkUserLogin(user)){
        removeOptionsMeliaRewards()
        usuario = user.token;
    }

    var promotionCode = '';

    if(typeof promotionCode !== 'undefined' && promotionCode !== null) {
        loadPromotionCode(promotionCode);
    }
}

function checkUserLogin(user) {
    return (null !== typeof user && undefined !== typeof user && user.token !== "");
}

function removeOptionsMeliaRewards() {
    $('.footer-content').empty();
}

function loadPromotionCode(promotionCode) {
    var currentTime = (new Date()).getTime(),
        endTime = currentTime + 1000 * 10,
        isAvailableObject;

    interval = setInterval(function () {
        isAvailableObject = !!too && !!too.be && !!too.be.promotion;
        if (isAvailableObject) {
            too.be.promotion.setCode(promotionCode);
        }

        if (isAvailableObject || new Date().getTime() > endTime) {
            clearInterval(interval);
        }

    }, 100);

}
  </script>
  <script>
   var templateRender = {
        startDelimiter: '{{',
        endDelimiter: '}}',

        fetch: function (url) {
            var result = '';
            var settings = {
                url : url,
                async : false
            };

            $.ajax(settings)
                .success(function (response) {
                    result = response;
                })
                .fail(function () {
                    console.error("Failed to get template.");
                });

            return result;
        },

        render: function (html, args) {

            var keys = Object.keys(args);
            var ret = html;

            for (index in keys) {
                var key = keys[index];
                var value = args[key];
                ret = ret.replace(new RegExp(this.startDelimiter + key + this.endDelimiter, 'g'), value);
            }

            return ret;
        }
    };
  </script>
  <script type="text/javascript">
   'use strict';

    const containerHtmlPopUpHome = '/booking/components/popUps/popUpLastSearch/popUpLastSearchHome.jsp';
    const containerHtmlPopUpHotelSheet = '/booking/components/popUps/popUpLastSearch/popUpLastSearchHotelSheet.jsp';
    const contentHtmlPopUp = '/booking/components/popUps/popUpLastSearch/dataPopUpLastSearch.jsp';
    const view = 'home';

    // Desactive PopUpLastSearch JS
    // executePopUpLastSearch();

    function executePopUpLastSearch() {
        $( document ).ready(function() {
            var currentHtmlLang = $('html')[0].lang;
            $.ajax({
                url : "/booking/components/popUps/popUpLastSearch/E_PopUpLastSearch.jsp?t=" + new Date().getTime(),
                type: "GET",
                data: {lang: currentHtmlLang},
                dataType: 'json',
                success : function(response) {
                    printResponseLastSearch(response);
                },
                error : function(response) {
                    procesErrorLastSearch(response);
                }
            });
        });
    }

    function procesErrorLastSearch(response){
        var responseText = response.responseText.trim();
        console.log("Response: " + response.statusText + " Code: " + response.status);
    }

    function printResponseLastSearch(jsonResponse) {

        if (jsonResponse.length > 0){

            var containerHtml = "";
            var finalContentHtml = "";

            if(view == "home"){
                 containerHtml = templateRender.render(templateRender.fetch(containerHtmlPopUpHome + "?t=" + new Date().getTime()), {copyTitle: jsonResponse[0].copyTitle});
            }else if(view == "hotelSheet"){
                 containerHtml = templateRender.render(templateRender.fetch(containerHtmlPopUpHotelSheet + "?t=" + new Date().getTime()), {copyTitle: jsonResponse[0].copyTitle});
            }

            var contentHtml = templateRender.fetch(contentHtmlPopUp + "?t=" + new Date().getTime());

            for (var i = 0; i < jsonResponse.length; i++) {
                let lastSearch = jsonResponse[i];
                var templateData = {
                    nombreDestino: lastSearch.nombreDestino,
                    fechaFormateada: lastSearch.fechaFormateada,
                    numNoches: lastSearch.noches,
                    noches: lastSearch.copyNoches,
                    numCookie: lastSearch.numCookie,
                    copyBotton: lastSearch.copyBotton,
                };
                finalContentHtml += templateRender.render(contentHtml, templateData);
            }

            if(finalContentHtml.length > 0 && $('.mbe-body').size() > 0) {

                if (view == "home") {
                    $('.mbe-body').prepend(containerHtml);
                } else if (view == "hotelSheet") {
                    $('.mbe-top-section').prepend(containerHtml);
                }

                $('#popUpUl').append(finalContentHtml);

                loadEventPopUpLastSearch();

            }

        }

    }

    function loadEventPopUpLastSearch() {

        $('.c-last-search-popup-new__close').on('click', function () {
            $(".c-last-search-popup-new").hide();
        });

        $('.c-last-search-popup-new li a').on('click', function () {
            loading("on");
            too.be.restore(parseInt($(this).attr('id')));
            if(too.be.destination.hotelList.length <= 0){
                setTimeout(function(){too.be.search();},500);
            }else{
                too.be.search();
            }
        });

        $('#mbe-destination-input').focus('click', function(){
            $(".c-last-search-popup-new").hide();
        });

    }
  </script>

        onClickInLowestPrice: function(e, idHotel){
            console.log('CLICK IN LOWEST MELIA BUTTON');
            var hotelName = $(e.currentTarget).parents(".lmm-main-box-hotel-detail-panel--hotel-detail-panel").find(".title-text a").text();
            var hotelCode = idHotel;
            selectedHotel = {name: hotelName, id: hotelCode};

            if(typeof isAMPMaps != "undefined") {
                window.top.location.href = "/booking/amp/components/C_Buscador.jsp?fHotel=true&codHotel=" + selectedHotel.id + "&tituloHotel=" + selectedHotel.name;
            } else {
                if(!!$("#too-be").length) {
                    openSearchHotelDir(e, selectedHotel);
                } else {
                    window.top.location.href = $(e.currentTarget).parents(".lmm-main-box-hotel-detail-panel--hotel-detail-panel").find(".title-text a").attr("href");;
                }
            }
        },
        onClickInRegularPrice: function(e, idHotel){
            console.log('CLICK IN REGULAR MELIA BUTTON');
            var hotelName = $(e.currentTarget).parents(".lmm-main-box-hotel-detail-panel--hotel-detail-panel").find(".title-text a").text();
            var hotelCode = idHotel;
            selectedHotel = {name: hotelName, id: hotelCode};

            if(typeof isAMPMaps != "undefined") {
                window.top.location.href = "/booking/amp/components/C_Buscador.jsp?fHotel=true&codHotel=" + selectedHotel.id + "&tituloHotel=" + selectedHotel.name;
            } else {
                if(!!$("#too-be").length) {
                    openSearchHotelDir(e, selectedHotel);
                } else {
                    window.top.location.href = $(e.currentTarget).parents(".lmm-main-box-hotel-detail-panel--hotel-detail-panel").find(".title-text a").attr("href");;
                }
            }
        }
    };

    function fProcessMapTab(){

        // $("#mapa-google-home").html("");
        if(control==0){
            setTimeout(function(){
                $("#mapa-google-home").show();
                jQuery('#mapa-google-home').width('100%');
                jQuery('#mapa-google-home').height('500px');

                /*var mapConfig = Object.assign(commonConfig, {
                    typeWidget: 'destinationsTree',
                    initialDestinationId: atributo
                });*/

                var mapConfig = commonConfig;
                mapConfig.typeWidget = "destinationsTree";
                mapConfig.initialDestinationId = atributo;

                mapConfig.hotels = {
                    alternativeHotelList: {
                        iconMarker: 'secondary-hotel-marker.svg'
                    }
                };

                lmmMapsWidget.createWidget('mapa-google-home', mapConfig, apiObject).then(function(widget) {
                    miMapaEmergia = widget;
                });
            },500);
            control=1;
        } else {
            miMapaEmergia.notify({
                type: 'REGION_CHANGED',
                object: {
                    regionId: atributo
                }
            });
        }
    }

    function changeCurrency(newCurrency){
        if(typeof miMapaEmergia!="undefined"){
            if(newCurrency.posicionSimbolo=="right"){
                commonConfig.currencyPrefix=true;
            }else{
                commonConfig.currencyPrefix=false;
            }
            miMapaEmergia.notify({
                type:'CURRENCY_CHANGED',
                object:{
                    currency:newCurrency.codigo,
                    currencySign:newCurrency.simbolo,
                    currencyPrefix:commonConfig.currencyPrefix
                }
            });
        }else{
            commonConfig.currency=newCurrency.codigo;
            commonConfig.currencySign=newCurrency.simbolo;
        }
    }

    var atributo="";
    var control=0;
    if($("#nav-continentes li.active a").attr("data-name")!=continente){
        $("#nav-continentes li").each(function(){
            if($(this).find("a").attr("data-name")==continente){
                $(this).find("a").click();
            }
        });
    }
    function obtenerCategory(name){
        var category;
        switch (name) {
            case "Europa":
                category="c6970521-2764-4885-9ead-1205dc96f784";
                break;
            case "Asia_Oceania":
                category="6d7837ae-edbb-467c-89c8-3cce3e6016ac";
                break;
            case "Africa_Oriente_Medio":
                category="700ab773-c68c-4aa9-a0d0-a1c1e1a6a23a";
                break;
            case "America":
                category="7f607c4b-a687-44db-9098-4ec699317b0b";
                break;
        }
        return category;
    }
    function initMap(nameContinent){
        if(miMapaEmergia==undefined){
            control=0;
        }
        atributo="mhi-destinations@"+obtenerCategory(nameContinent);
        //loadGoogleAPI(fProcessMapTab);
        try{
            if(simbolosMonedas[commonConfig.currency].posicionSimbolo=="right" && typeof simbolosMonedas!="undefined"){
                commonConfig.currencyPrefix=true;
            }else{
                commonConfig.currencyPrefix=false;
            }
        }catch(e){
            console.log(e);
        }
        fProcessMapTab();
    }

    $("#nav-continentes li").click(function(){
        name=$(this).find('a').attr("data-name");
        if(typeof miMapaEmergia!="undefined") {
            initMap(name);
        }
    });

    function Moneda(codigo, simbolo, factor, descripcion, position){
        this.codigo = codigo;
        this.simbolo = simbolo;
        this.factor = factor;
        this.descripcion = descripcion;
        this.posicionSimbolo = position;
    }

    // Simbolos de moneda
    simbolosMonedas = new Array();
    
    simbolosMonedas['VND'] = new Moneda('VND','₫','0.000036', 'nReservas.CURRENCY_DESCRIPTION_VND', 'left');
    
    simbolosMonedas['IDR'] = new Moneda('IDR','Rp','0.000058', 'nReservas.CURRENCY_DESCRIPTION_IDR', 'left');

    simbolosMonedas['BRL'] = new Moneda('BRL','R$','0.149370', 'nReservas.CURRENCY_DESCRIPTION_BRL', 'left');
    
    simbolosMonedas['AED'] = new Moneda('AED','AED','0.227410', 'nReservas.CURRENCY_DESCRIPTION_AED', 'right');
    
    simbolosMonedas['AUD'] = new Moneda('AUD','AU$','0.653940', 'nReservas.CURRENCY_DESCRIPTION_AUD', 'left');
    
    simbolosMonedas['USD'] = new Moneda('USD','$','0.835280', 'nReservas.CURRENCY_DESCRIPTION_USD', 'left');
    
    simbolosMonedas['CHF'] = new Moneda('CHF','SFr','0.904450', 'nReservas.CURRENCY_DESCRIPTION_CHF', '');
    
    simbolosMonedas['EUR'] = new Moneda('EUR','€','1.000000', 'nReservas.CURRENCY_DESCRIPTION_EUR', 'right');
    
    simbolosMonedas['GBP'] = new Moneda('GBP','£','1.167720', 'nReservas.CURRENCY_DESCRIPTION_GBP', 'left');
    

    /* Precio desde en destinos */
    var codigoMoneda = 'USD';
    if(simboloMoneda !== undefined) {
        $("#desdeSimbolo").text(simboloMoneda);
    }
    var monedaPred = "";

    if(codigoMoneda != "*") {
        monedaPred = simbolosMonedas[codigoMoneda];
    } else {
        monedaPred = simbolosMonedas["USD"];
    }

    var precioDesde = $(".caption #desdePrecio").text();
    if(null != monedaPred && typeof monedaPred != undefined && typeof precioDesde != undefined) {
        try {
            var precio = (precioDesde * monedaPred.factor) / monedaPred.factor;
            //Cogemos el entero superior mas cercano.
            precio = Math.round(precio);
            var simboloMoneda = monedaPred.simbolo;
            var posicionMoneda = monedaPred.posicionSimbolo;
            var precioFormateado = "";
            if(posicionMoneda != "left") {
                precioFormateado = precio + simboloMoneda;
            } else {
                precioFormateado = simboloMoneda + " " + precio;
            }

            if(precioFormateado != "" && precio > 0) {
                var mostrar = $(".caption #desdeFormateado").text(precioFormateado);
                mostrar.parent().find("span:not(#desdeFormateado)").remove();
            }else{
                //TODO: remove price references.
                var mostrar = $(".caption #desdeFormateado");
                mostrar.parent().parent().find("small").remove();
                mostrar.parent().remove();
            }
        }catch(e) {
            $(".caption #desdePrecio").text(precioDesde.replace(".00", ""));
            var mostrar = $(".caption #desdeFormateado");
            mostrar.parent().parent().find("small").remove();
            mostrar.parent().remove();
            console.log("No se ha podido recuperar asignar el precio formateado");
        }
    } else {
        var mostrar = $(".caption #desdeFormateado");
        mostrar.parent().parent().find("small").remove();
        mostrar.parent().remove();
    }

    var langUrl = 'en_us';
    var hotelesProp = 'hotels';
    popUpHome = $(".map-hotel .price-popup");

    if(typeof isAMPMaps != "undefined") {
        /*var mapConfig = Object.assign(commonConfig, {
            typeWidget: 'destinationsTree',
            initialDestinationId: uidCategoria
        });*/

        var mapConfig = commonConfig;
        mapConfig.typeWidget = "destinationsTree";
        mapConfig.initialDestinationId = uidCategoria;


        mapConfig.hotels = {
            alternativeHotelList: {
                iconMarker: 'secondary-hotel-marker.svg'
            }
        };
        mapConfig.mobileVersion = true;

        /* Fallo al recuperar variables de sesión */
        if(mapConfig.currency == "") {
            mapConfig.currency = currencyMap;
        }
        if(mapConfig.currencySign == "") {
            mapConfig.currencySign = currencySignMap;
        }

        lmmMapsWidget.createWidget('mapa-google', mapConfig, apiObject);
    }

    function openSearchHotelDir(e, hotel){
        if (hotel == undefined){
            hotel = selectedHotel;
        }

        too.be.destination.setHotel(hotel.name, hotel.id, true);
        $('.mbe-dates:not(.open) .mbe-input-dates').click();
        e.stopPropagation();
    }

   function getCopiesForLibJs(){
       var copies = {};
       copies["cuentacasa"] = "House Account";
       copies["bcc"] = "HAV";
       copies["invitado"] = "Guest";
       copies["exceeded"] = "Exceeded the maximum number of rooms to reserve.";
       return copies;
   }

  <script>
   /* BUSCADOR */
	var circlePattern = new RegExp("/circle/|circlebymelia.com");
	

	/* Por el function.js */
	if (typeof too != 'undefined'  &&  typeof too.be == 'undefined' )
		too.be = new TooBe();

	$(document).ready(function() {
        too.be.loadCopies(getCopiesForLibJs());
        fillBeneficiaryInSearcher(too.be);
		too.be.load();
        var isTablet = 'true' === 'false';
        var isMobile = 'true' === '';
        if (!isTablet && !isMobile) {
		too.be.setActive(true);
        }
		too.be.flexCalendar.setActive(false);
		var dat = new Date();
		var checkIn = new Date(dat.getFullYear(), dat.getMonth(), dat.getDate(), dat.getHours(), dat.getMinutes(), dat.getSeconds(), dat.getMilliseconds());
		too.be.calendar.drawDates();
		too.be.setTopPosition(50);
        too.be.setTopPositionMobile(50);

		if (typeof bEsFichaHotel != "undefined" && (bEsFichaHotel.constructor !== Boolean || bEsFichaHotel == true)) {
			too.be.destination.setHotel(tituloSinNormalizar, codigoHotelFicha, false);
			var precioHotel = '';
			if (typeof precioHotel != 'undefined' && precioHotel !== undefined && precioHotel !== null && precioHotel !== "" ) {
				too.be.destination.setBookFrom(precioHotel);
			}else{
				$('.bookFromOnly').css('display','none');
			}
			too.be.close();
		}
		var promotionCode = '';
		if(typeof promotionCode !== 'undefined' && promotionCode !== null && promotionCode !== "") {
    	    too.be.promotion.setCode(promotionCode);
            too.be.open();
	    }
		var rateRequest = '';
		if(typeof rateRequest !== 'undefined' && rateRequest !== null) {
			too.be.setRateRequest(rateRequest);
	    }
		var fechaEntrada = '';
		var fechaSalida = '';
        if(fechaEntrada!== null && fechaEntrada !== "" && fechaSalida!== null && fechaSalida !== "") {
            var dateEntrada = new Date(fechaEntrada * 1000);
            var dateSalida = new Date(fechaSalida * 1000);
            if(dateEntrada !== undefined && dateEntrada !== null && dateSalida !== undefined && dateSalida !== null) {
                var formatDateEntrada = formatFecha(dateEntrada);
                var formatDateSalida = formatFecha(dateSalida);
            }
        }
    	if(typeof formatDateEntrada !== 'undefined' && formatDateEntrada !== null && typeof formatDateSalida !== 'undefined' && formatDateSalida !== null) {
    		too.be.calendar.setCheckIn(formatDateEntrada.toString());
    		too.be.calendar.setCheckOut(formatDateSalida.toString());
    		too.be.calendar.drawDates();

            var paramCheckinDate = "fechaEntrada=" + fechaEntrada;
            var paramCheckoutDate = "fechaSalida=" + fechaSalida;
            var promotionCode;

            

            addParametersToListLanguages(getParametersUrl(paramCheckinDate, paramCheckoutDate, promotionCode));
	    }

        fillOccupationInSearcher(too.be);

        
	});

	if (!document.referrer.match(circlePattern)
			&& !document.location.host.match(circlePattern)) {
		$("#too-be").removeClass("hidden");
	} else {
		$(".c-hotel-sheet-rewards-promo strong").hide();
	}

	function formatFecha(date) {
		var anyo = date.getFullYear();
		var mes = date.getMonth();
		var dia = date.getDate();
		return new Date(anyo, mes, dia, 12, 0, 0);
	}

	function getParametersUrl() {
	    var params = "?";
        for(var i = 0; i < arguments.length; i++) {
            var param = arguments[i];
            if(param !== '' && typeof param !== 'undefined') {
                if(i === 0) {
                    params += arguments[i]
                } else {
                    params += "&" + arguments[i];
                }
            }
        }

        return params;
    }

    function addParametersToListLanguages(parameters) {
        $('#menuLanguages a.line').each(function() {
            var element = $(this);
            var hrefValue = element.attr('href');
            if(hrefValue !== '#') {
                hrefValue += parameters;
                element.attr('href', hrefValue);
            }
        });
    }

    function fillOccupationInSearcher(searcher) {
        searcher.rooms.reset();

        

        searcher.rooms.draw();
    }

    function fillBeneficiaryInSearcher(searcher) {
        searcher.setBookingType('');
        searcher.setBeneficiaryName(' ');
    }

    function fillCorporateCodeInSearcher(searcher) {
        searcher.promotion.setCode('');
    }
